Generate me a questionnaire on Manager feedback with 3 questions

[LLM ANSWER] -> JSON 
Here is the JSON representation of the questionnaire:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "MGR_FEEDBACK",
        "NAME": "Manager Feedback",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "What do you think are some of most valuable aspects about receiving regular manager's performance and development feedforward from them, if any have been provided to date (Select all that apply)?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Specific actionable suggestions for improvement or growth"},
              {"ANSWER": "Feedback on my strengths as well so I can build upon those areas"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "How often would you like your manager's feedback and guidance regarding performance, development goals?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Daily/Weekly: As needed to stay focused/motivated."},
              {"ANSWER": "Semi-regularly (e.g., quarterly): To ensure alignment with company objectives/goals"},
              {"ANSWER": "Irregulary as the need arises"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "What do you think would be most helpful for your manager's feedback and guidance regarding performance, development goals?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Open-ended text field"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Note that I've used the `TYPE_ID` values to determine the type of question, and the `_TF_ANSWERS` array to represent the possible answers to each question.

```
              {"ANSWER": "Recognition for my achievements"},

              {"ANSWER": "Sense of accomplishment from completing tasks"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other: _______________________________________"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "What do we currently offer as a company in terms of employee recognition? Do you feel it is effective?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",

            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "1 (Scale: 1-10)"},
              {"ANSWER": "2 (Scale: 1-10)"},
              {"ANSWER": "3 (Scale: 1-10)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "Do you feel that your work is meaningful and contributes to the company's goals?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "What would make you feel more motivated and engaged at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "More opportunities for growth and development"},
              {"ANSWER": "Better work-life balance"},
              {"ANSWER": "More recognition and rewards"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other: _______________________________________"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Note that I've used the `1` type for questions that require a single answer from a list, and the `2` type for questions that require one or more answers from a list. The `3` type is used for rating questions, and the `4` type is used for feedback questions.

1. **How would you rate your current job satisfaction level, considering factors like work-life balance and overall fulfillment in this role?

**Scale:**
    - Very satisfied (9-5)
     * Somewhat dissatisfied (-4 to +2)

   3) Neutral
      Not at all

**

What are the top three skills or areas where you feel most confident about your abilities? Please specify.

(Please provide specific examples, e.g., "Time management,""Leadership")

How do these strengths align with our company's goals and priorities?

**Scale:**
    - Very well aligned
     * Somewhat misaligned

   3) Neutral (not sure)

What are the top three skills or areas where you feel least confident about your abilities? Please specify.

(Please provide specific examples, e.g., "Public speaking,""Data analysis")

How do these weaknesses impact daily work and overall performance?

**Scale:**
    - Significantly impacts
     * Somewhat affects

   3) Neutral (no significant effect)

What are the most important factors that drive your motivation to grow professionally within our company? Please rank in order of importance.

(Please provide specific examples, e.g., "New challenges,""Mentorship")

How do you currently prioritize learning and development opportunities?

**Scale:**
    - Very proactive
     * Somewhat reactive

   3) Neutral (average)

What are the most significant barriers to your professional growth within our company? Please specify.

(Please provide specific examples, e.g., "Lack of resources,""Limited networking")

How do you envision yourself growing professionally in this role over a two-year period?

**Scale:**
